Design Principles\n    14→\n    15→1. **Structural-first**: ~70% of checks are deterministic Python; LLM handles only the residual semantic 30%.\n    16→2. **Immutable data flow**: Parsers produce frozen dataclasses; checkers return new `Finding` lists — no shared mutable state.\n    17→3. **Registry-centric gate**: The convergence gate reads the deviation registry, never raw scan output. `SPEC_FIDELITY_GATE` is excluded from convergence mode to prevent dual-authority conflicts (see Sec 5.3).\n    18→4. **Backward compatibility**: Pipeline steps 1–7 are untouched. The new system replaces step 8 (`spec-fidelity`) internals and adds post-step-8 orchestration.\n    19→5. **Minimal new files**: 5 new modules, 2 modified modules. No new CLI commands.\n    20→\n    21→---\n    22→\n    23→## 2. Module Map\n    24→\n    25→### 2.1 New Modules\n    26→\n    27→| Module | Location | Responsibility | FR |\n    28→|--------|----------|----------------|----|\n    29→| `spec_parser.py` | `cli/roadmap/spec_parser.py` | Parse spec + roadmap into structured `SpecData` / `RoadmapData` | FR-2 |\n    30→| `structural_checkers.py` | `cli/roadmap/structural_checkers.py` | 5 checker callables + registry + severity rule tables | FR-1, FR-3 |\n    31→| `semantic_layer.py` | `cli/roadmap/semantic_layer.py` | Chunked LLM residual pass + adversarial debate hook | FR-4, FR-5 |\n    32→| `deviation_registry.py` | `cli/roadmap/deviation_registry.py` | File-backed JSON registry with stable IDs, run metadata | FR-6, FR-10 |\n    33→| `convergence.py` | `cli/roadmap/convergence.py` | 3-run budget, monotonic progress (structural_high_count only), regression detection | FR-7, FR-8 |\n    34→\n    35→### 2.2 Modified Modules\n    36→\n    37→| Module | Change | FR |\n    38→|--------|--------|----|\n    39→| `executor.py` | Replace `spec-fidelity` step construction; add convergence loop after step 8 | FR-7 |\n    40→| `remediate_executor.py` | Add MorphLLM patch format + diff-size guard + fallback applicator | FR-9 |\n    41→\n    42→### 2.3 Unchanged Modules\n    43→\n    44→Steps 1–7 (`prompts.py` build_extract/generate/diff/debate/score/merge/test_strategy), `gates.py` (existing gate definitions), `fidelity.py` (Severity enum + FidelityDeviation — retained, extended), `spec_patch.py` (accepted deviation workflow), `models.py` (Finding dataclass — extended, not replaced).\n    45→\n    46→---\n    47→\n    48→## 3. Data Model\n    49→\n    50→### 3.1 Spec Parser Output (`spec_parser.py`)\n    51→\n    52→```python\n    53→from __future__ import annotations\n    54→from dataclasses import dataclass, field\n    55→from typing import Literal\n    56→\n    57→@dataclass(frozen=True)\n    58→class FunctionSignature:\n    59→    \"\"\"Extracted Python function signature from fenced code block.\"\"\"\n    60→    name: str\n    61→    params: list[str]           # parameter names (no types)\n    62→    return_type: str | None     # return annotation string or None\n    63→    source_section: str         # heading path where found, e.g. \"3.1/FR-1\"\n    64→\n    65→@dataclass(frozen=True)\n    66→class RequirementID:\n    67→    \"\"\"A requirement identifier extracted from spec text.\"\"\"\n    68→    id: str                     # e.g. \"FR-1.2\", \"NFR-3\", \"SC-1\", \"G-2\", \"D5\"\n    69→    family: str                 # e.g. \"FR\", \"NFR\", \"SC\", \"G\", \"D\"\n    70→    source_section: str\n    71→\n    72→@dataclass(frozen=True)\n    73→class FileManifestEntry:\n    74→    \"\"\"A file path from a spec manifest table (Sec 4.1, 4.2, 4.3).\"\"\"\n    75→    path: str                   # e.g. \"src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/spec_parser.py\"\n    76→    description: str\n    77→    source_section: str\n    78→\n    79→@dataclass(frozen=True)\n    80→class ThresholdExpression:\n    81→    \"\"\"A numeric threshold from spec text, e.g. '< 5s', '>= 90%'.\"\"\"\n    82→    raw: str                    # original text\n    83→    operator: str               # '<', '<=', '>', '>=', '=='\n    84→    value: float\n    85→    unit: str                   # 's', '%', 'KB', '' etc.\n    86→    source_section: str\n    87→\n    88→@dataclass(frozen=True)\n    89→class EnumLiteral:\n    90→    \"\"\"A Literal[...] enum value extracted from a fenced code block.\"\"\"\n    91→    type_name: str              # e.g. \"enforcement_tier\"\n    92→    values: tuple[str, ...]     # e.g. (\"STRICT\", \"STANDARD\", \"LIGHT\", \"EXEMPT\")\n    93→    source_section: str\n    94→\n    95→@dataclass(frozen=True)\n    96→class CrossReference:\n    97→    \"\"\"A cross-section reference extracted from spec text.\"\"\"\n    98→    from_section: str           # section containing the reference\n    99→    to_section: str             # section being referenced\n   100→    context: str                # surrounding text snippet\n   101→\n   102→@dataclass(frozen=True)\n   103→class SpecSection:\n   104→    \"\"\"A parsed top-level section of the spec.\"\"\"\n   105→    heading: str                # e.g. \"3. Functional Requirements\"\n   106→    heading_path: str           # e.g. \"3\"\n   107→    level: int                  # heading level (2 = ##)\n   108→    content: str                # raw markdown content\n   109→    byte_size: int              # len(content.encode('utf-8'))\n   110→\n   111→@dataclass(frozen=True)\n   112→class SpecData:\n   113→    \"\"\"Complete structured extraction from a spec document.\"\"\"\n   114→    frontmatter: dict[str, str]\n   115→    sections: tuple[SpecSection, ...]\n   116→    signatures: tuple[FunctionSignature, ...]\n   117→    requirement_ids: tuple[RequirementID, ...]\n   118→    file_manifest: tuple[FileManifestEntry, ...]\n   119→    thresholds: tuple[ThresholdExpression, ...]\n   120→    enum_literals: tuple[EnumLiteral, ...]\n   121→    cross_references: tuple[CrossReference, ...]\n   122→\n   123→    # Derived lookup indexes (computed in __post_init__ of mutable builder)\n   124→    section_by_heading: dict[str, SpecSection] = field(default_factory=dict)\n   125→    ids_by_family: dict[str, frozenset[str]] = field(default_factory=dict)\n   126→\n   127→@dataclass(frozen=True)\n   128→class RoadmapData:\n   129→    \"\"\"Structured extraction from a roadmap document.\"\"\"\n   130→    frontmatter: dict[str, str]\n   131→    sections: tuple[SpecSection, ...]      # reuse SpecSection for heading+content\n   132→    referenced_ids: frozenset[str]         # all FR-*, NFR-*, etc. found in text\n   133→    file_paths: frozenset[str]             # all file paths found in tasks\n   134→    function_names: frozenset[str]         # function/method names in task descriptions\n   135→    field_references: frozenset[str]       # dataclass field names referenced\n   136→    gate_params: frozenset[str]            # Step(...) parameter names referenced\n   137→```\n   138→\n   139→**Parser functions** (all pure, no I/O beyond reading the two input files):\n   140→\n   141→```python\n   142→def parse_spec(spec_path: Path) -> SpecData: ...\n   143→def parse_roadmap(roadmap_path: Path) -> RoadmapData: ...\n   144→```\n   145→\n   146→**Implementation notes**:\n   147→- YAML frontmatter: `yaml.safe_load` on `---` delimited block (reuse `_extract_frontmatter` pattern from `spec_patch.py`)\n   148→- Markdown tables: regex split on `|` with header row detection\n   149→- Fenced code blocks: `^```python` … `^```\\n` regex, then `ast.parse` for signatures\n   150→- Requirement IDs: `re.findall(r'(?:FR|NFR|SC|G|D)-?\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)*', text)`\n   151→- `Literal[...]`: regex on `Literal\\[([^\\]]+)\\]` within fenced blocks\n   152→- Thresholds: regex `(<=?|>=?|==)\\s*([\\d.]+)\\s*(%|s|ms|KB|MB|)?`\n   153→- Cross-references: regex for `See (?:section |§)(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)*)` and `FR-\\d+` in non-home sections\n   154→- Section splitting: `^## \\d+\\.` regex on spec; `^## ` on roadmap\n   155→\n   156→---\n   157→\n   158→### 3.2 Structural Finding Model\n   159→\n   160→Extends the existing `Finding` dataclass in `models.py`:\n   161→\n   162→```python\n   163→# Addition to models.py (or new field in Finding)\n   164→# No new class needed — Finding already has all required fields.\n   165→# New fields added:\n   166→\n   167→@dataclass\n   168→class Finding:\n   169→    # ... existing fields ...\n   170→    rule_id: str = \"\"           # e.g. \"SIG-MISSING-FUNC\", \"DM-PATH-PREFIX\"\n   171→    spec_quote: str = \"\"        # verbatim spec text\n   172→    roadmap_quote: str = \"\"     # verbatim roadmap text or \"[MISSING]\"\n   173→    stable_id: str = \"\"         # hash-derived ID for registry dedup\n   174→```\n   175→\n   176→**Stable ID derivation** (FR-6):\n   177→\n   178→```python\n   179→import hashlib\n   180→\n   181→def compute_stable_id(\n   182→    dimension: str,\n   183→    rule_id: str,\n   184→    spec_location: str,\n   185→    mismatch_type: str,\n   186→) -> str:\n   187→    \"\"\"Deterministic finding ID from structural properties.\"\"\"\n   188→    key = f\"{dimension}:{rule_id}:{spec_location}:{mismatch_type}\"\n   189→    return hashlib.sha256(key.encode()).hexdigest()[:16]\n   190→```\n   191→\n   192→---\n   193→\n   194→### 3.3 Severity Rule Table Schema\n   195→\n   196→```python\n   197→from dataclasses import dataclass\n   198→from typing import Literal as Lit\n   199→\n   200→SeverityLevel = Lit[\"HIGH\", \"MEDIUM\", \"LOW\"]\n   201→\n   202→@dataclass(frozen=True)\n   203→class SeverityRule:\n   204→    \"\"\"One row in a checker's severity rule table.\"\"\"\n   205→    dimension: str          # e.g. \"signatures\"\n   206→    mismatch_type: str      # e.g. \"function_missing\"\n   207→    severity: SeverityLevel\n   208→    description: str        # human-readable rule description\n   209→\n   210→# Type alias for the rule table\n   211→SeverityRuleTable = dict[str, SeverityLevel]  # key: mismatch_type -> severity\n   212→```\n   213→\n   214→---\n   215→\n   216→## 4. Component Architecture\n   217→\n   218→### 4.1 Spec Parser (`spec_parser.py`)\n   219→\n   220→**Responsibility**: FR-2. Read spec and roadmap files, return `SpecData` and `RoadmapData`.\n   221→\n   222→```\n   223→Input:  spec_path: Path, roadmap_path: Path\n   224→Output: SpecData, RoadmapData\n   225→I/O:    Reads 2 files (the only I/O in the entire checker pipeline)\n   226→```\n   227→\n   228→**Key design decisions**:\n   229→- **Single point of file I/O**: All downstream components receive parsed data, never file paths.\n   230→- **Frozen dataclasses**: Parser output is immutable — checkers cannot accidentally mutate shared state (NFR-4).\n   231→- **Section-level chunking**: Each `SpecSection` tracks its byte size for prompt budgeting (NFR-3).\n   232→- **Reference graph**: `cross_references` enables supplementary section injection per checker.\n   233→\n   234→**Section→Dimension mapping** (FR-5):\n   235→\n   236→```python\n   237→# Static mapping: which spec sections feed which checker dimension\n   238→DIMENSION_SECTIONS: dict[str, list[str]] = {\n   239→    \"signatures\":  [\"3\"],           # Sec 3: Functional Requirements\n   240→    \"data_models\": [\"4.1\", \"4.2\", \"4.3\"],  # Sec 4: File manifests\n   241→    \"gates\":       [\"3\", \"4\"],      # FR + data model gates\n   242→    \"cli\":         [\"5.1\"],         # Sec 5: CLI options\n   243→    \"nfrs\":        [\"6\"],           # Sec 6: Non-functional requirements\n   244→}\n   245→\n   246→def get_sections_for_dimension(\n   247→    dimension: str,\n   248→    spec: SpecData,\n   249→) -> list[SpecSection]:\n   250→    \"\"\"Return primary + supplementary sections for a checker dimension.\n   251→\n   252→    Primary sections come from DIMENSION_SECTIONS.\n   253→    Supplementary sections come from cross_references that link\n   254→    from primary sections to other sections.\n   255→    \"\"\"\n   256→```\n   257→\n   258→---\n   259→\n   260→### 4.2 Structural Checkers (`structural_checkers.py`)\n   261→\n   262→**Responsibility**: FR-1, FR-3. Five independent checker callables, each producing `list[Finding]`.\n   263→\n   264→#### 4.2.1 Checker Protocol\n   265→\n   266→```python\n   267→from typing import Protocol\n   268→\n   269→class StructuralChecker(Protocol):\n   270→    \"\"\"Protocol for all structural checkers.\"\"\"\n   271→\n   272→    dimension: str\n   273→    rules: SeverityRuleTable\n   274→\n   275→    def check(self, spec: SpecData, roadmap: RoadmapData) -> list[Finding]:\n   276→        \"\"\"Run deterministic checks, return findings with rule-based severity.\"\"\"\n   277→        ...\n   278→```\n   279→\n   280→#### 4.2.2 Five Checker Implementations\n   281→\n   282→**1. SignatureChecker** (dimension: `\"signatures\"`, ~80% structural)\n   283→\n   284→```python\n   285→class SignatureChecker:\n   286→    dimension = \"signatures\"\n   287→    rules: SeverityRuleTable = {\n   288→        \"phantom_id\":        \"HIGH\",    # Roadmap references ID not in spec\n   289→        \"function_missing\":  \"HIGH\",    # Spec function absent from roadmap\n   290→        \"param_arity\":       \"MEDIUM\",  # Parameter count mismatch\n   291→        \"id_missing\":        \"MEDIUM\",  # Spec ID not referenced in roadmap\n   292→    }\n   293→\n   294→    def check(self, spec: SpecData, roadmap: RoadmapData) -> list[Finding]:\n   295→        findings = []\n   296→        # 1. Phantom ID check: roadmap IDs ⊄ spec IDs\n   297→        spec_ids = set()\n   298→        for req in spec.requirement_ids:\n   299→            spec_ids.add(req.id)\n   300→        phantom = roadmap.referenced_ids - spec_ids\n   301→        for pid in sorted(phantom):\n   302→            findings.append(Finding(\n   303→                dimension=self.dimension,\n   304→                rule_id=\"phantom_id\",\n   305→                severity=\"HIGH\",\n   306→                ...\n   307→            ))\n   308→        # 2. Missing function check\n   309→        # 3. Parameter arity check\n   310→        return findings\n   311→```\n   312→\n   313→**2. DataModelChecker** (dimension: `\"data_models\"`, ~85% structural)\n   314→\n   315→```python\n   316→rules = {\n   317→    \"file_missing\":      \"HIGH\",    # Required spec file missing from roadmap\n   318→    \"path_prefix\":       \"HIGH\",    # File path prefix mismatch\n   319→    \"enum_uncovered\":    \"MEDIUM\",  # Enum literal not covered\n   320→    \"field_missing\":     \"MEDIUM\",  # Dataclass field not referenced\n   321→}\n   322→```\n   323→\n   324→**3. GateChecker** (dimension: `\"gates\"`, ~65% structural)\n   325→\n   326→```python\n   327→rules = {\n   328→    \"frontmatter_field\": \"HIGH\",    # Required frontmatter field not covered\n   329→    \"step_param\":        \"MEDIUM\",  # Step parameter missing\n   330→    \"ordering\":          \"MEDIUM\",  # Ordering constraint violated\n   331→}\n   332→```\n   333→\n   334→**4. CLIChecker** (dimension: `\"cli\"`, ~75% structural)\n   335→\n   336→```python\n   337→rules = {\n   338→    \"mode_uncovered\":    \"MEDIUM\",  # Config mode not covered\n   339→    \"default_mismatch\":  \"MEDIUM\",  # Default value mismatch\n   340→}\n   341→```\n   342→\n   343→**5. NFRChecker** (dimension: `\"nfrs\"`, ~55% structural)\n   344→\n   345→```python\n   346→rules = {\n   347→    \"threshold_contradicted\": \"HIGH\",    # Numeric threshold contradicted\n   348→    \"security_missing\":       \"HIGH\",    # Security primitive missing\n   349→    \"dependency_violated\":    \"HIGH\",    # Dependency direction violated\n   350→    \"coverage_mismatch\":      \"MEDIUM\",  # Coverage threshold mismatch\n   351→}\n   352→```\n   353→\n   354→#### 4.2.3 Checker Registry\n   355→\n   356→```python\n   357→# Module-level registry\n   358→CHECKER_REGISTRY: dict[str, StructuralChecker] = {\n   359→    \"signatures\":  SignatureChecker(),\n   360→    \"data_models\": DataModelChecker(),\n   361→    \"gates\":       GateChecker(),\n   362→    \"cli\":         CLIChecker(),\n   363→    \"nfrs\":        NFRChecker(),\n   364→}\n   365→\n   366→def run_all_checkers(\n   367→    spec: SpecData,\n   368→    roadmap: RoadmapData,\n   369→) -> list[Finding]:\n   370→    \"\"\"Execute all checkers in parallel, merge findings.\"\"\"\n   371→    from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed\n   372→\n   373→    all_findings: list[Finding] = []\n   374→    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as pool:\n   375→        futures = {\n   376→            pool.submit(checker.check, spec, roadmap): dim\n   377→            for dim, checker in CHECKER_REGISTRY.items()\n   378→        }\n   379→        for future in as_completed(futures):\n   380→            all_findings.extend(future.result())\n   381→\n   382→    # Assign stable IDs\n   383→    for f in all_findings:\n   384→        f.stable_id = compute_stable_id(\n   385→            f.dimension, f.rule_id, f.location, f.rule_id\n   386→        )\n   387→\n   388→    return all_findings\n   389→```\n   390→\n   391→**Key design decisions**:\n   392→- **ThreadPoolExecutor** not ProcessPoolExecutor: checkers are CPU-light (string matching), not CPU-bound. Thread pool avoids serialization overhead.\n   393→- **No shared mutable state**: Each checker receives the same frozen `SpecData`/`RoadmapData` and returns its own list (NFR-4).\n   394→- **Rule tables in code**: `SeverityRuleTable` dicts are module-level constants, not prompt text (FR-3).\n   395→\n   396→---\n   397→\n   398→### 4.3 Residual Semantic Layer (`semantic_layer.py`)\n   399→\n   400→**Responsibility**: FR-4, FR-5. LLM-based checking for the ~30% that structural checkers can't handle.\n   401→\n   402→```python\n   403→@dataclass\n   404→class SemanticCheckRequest:\n   405→    \"\"\"Input to the semantic LLM layer for one dimension.\"\"\"\n   406→    dimension: str\n   407→    spec_sections: list[SpecSection]        # primary + supplementary\n   408→    roadmap_sections: list[SpecSection]\n   409→    structural_findings: list[Finding]      # context to avoid re-checking\n   410→    prior_findings_summary: str             # FR-10: run-to-run memory\n   411→\n   412→def build_semantic_prompt(request: SemanticCheckRequest) -> str:\n   413→    \"\"\"Build a chunked prompt for one semantic check.\n   414→\n   415→    Enforces NFR-3: prompt size ≤ 30KB.\n   416→    Includes structural findings as \"already checked\" context.\n   417→    Includes prior findings summary (max 50 entries) for anchoring.\n   418→    \"\"\"\n   419→\n   420→def run_semantic_layer(\n   421→    spec: SpecData,\n   422→    roadmap: RoadmapData,\n   423→    structural_findings: list[Finding],\n   424→    registry: DeviationRegistry,\n   425→    config: PipelineConfig,\n   426→) -> list[Finding]:\n   427→    \"\"\"Execute semantic checks per dimension, with adversarial debate for HIGHs.\n   428→\n   429→    Flow:\n   430→    1. For each dimension, build SemanticCheckRequest with only uncovered aspects\n   431→    2. Spawn ClaudeProcess with chunked prompt (≤30KB)\n   432→    3. Parse LLM output into Finding list\n   433→    4. For any Finding with severity HIGH:\n   434→       a. Spawn adversarial debate (lightweight variant)\n   435→       b. Debate produces verdict: CONFIRM_HIGH | DOWNGRADE_TO_MEDIUM | DOWNGRADE_TO_LOW\n   436→       c. Apply verdict, record debate transcript reference\n   437→    5. Return all semantic findings with final severities\n   438→    \"\"\"\n   439→```\n   440→\n   441→**Adversarial debate integration** (FR-4):\n   442→\n   443→```python\n   444→def validate_semantic_high(\n   445→    finding: Finding,\n   446→    spec_sections: list[SpecSection],\n   447→    roadmap_sections: list[SpecSection],\n   448→    config: PipelineConfig,\n   449→) -> tuple[str, str]:\n   450→    \"\"\"Spawn adversarial debate for a semantic HIGH finding.\n   451→\n   452→    Returns (verdict, transcript_reference):\n   453→        verdict: \"CONFIRM_HIGH\" | \"DOWNGRADE_TO_MEDIUM\" | \"DOWNGRADE_TO_LOW\"\n   454→        transcript_reference: path to debate output file\n   455→\n   456→    **Protocol**: Single-round prosecutor/defender with automated deterministic judge.\n   457→\n   458→    **Roles**:\n   459→    - Prosecutor (LLM): argues finding IS high severity\n   460→    - Defender (LLM): argues finding should be downgraded\n   461→    - Judge (Python): deterministic rubric scoring, no LLM call\n   462→\n   463→    **Rubric weights**:\n   464→    - Evidence quality: 30%\n   465→    - Impact specificity: 25%\n   466→    - Logical coherence: 25%\n   467→    - Concession handling: 20%\n   468→\n   469→    **Verdict thresholds**:\n   470→    - Prosecutor margin > 0.15 → CONFIRM_HIGH\n   471→    - Defender margin > 0.15 → DOWNGRADE_TO_{defender's recommendation}\n   472→    - Margin ≤ 0.15 (tiebreak) → CONFIRM_HIGH (conservative)\n   473→\n   474→    **Token budget**: ~3,800 tokens per finding (cap: 5,000)\n   475→    **LLM calls**: 2 per finding (prosecutor + defender, parallelized)\n   476→    \"\"\"\n   477→```\n   478→\n   479→**Key design decisions**:\n   480→- **Per-dimension chunking**: Each semantic check receives only its relevant sections, not the full documents (NFR-3).\n   481→- **Structural findings as negative context**: The prompt says \"the following have already been checked structurally — do NOT re-report them\", preventing double-counting.\n   482→- **Lightweight debate for semantic HIGHs**: Uses a streamlined 2-agent format (not full `/sc:adversarial`), reducing token cost while preserving adversarial validation.\n   483→- **FR-8 regression debate**: Uses full `/sc:adversarial` for consolidated post-regression findings. Regression is only triggered by increases in `structural_high_count`; semantic fluctuations are logged as warnings but never trigger regression.\n   484→\n   485→#### 4.3.1 Prompt Budget Enforcement (NFR-3)\n   486→\n   487→**Budget**: `MAX_PROMPT_BYTES = 30,720` (30KB)\n   488→\n   489→**Proportional allocation**:\n   490→| Component | Budget % | Bytes |\n   491→|-----------|----------|-------|\n   492→| Spec + roadmap sections | 60% | 18,432 |\n   493→| Structural findings context | 20% | 6,144 |\n   494→| Prior findings summary | 15% | 4,608 |\n   495→| Prompt template overhead | 5% | 1,536 |\n   496→\n   497→**Overflow handling**: Tail-truncation on line boundaries with `[TRUNCATED: N bytes omitted]` marker.\n   498→\n   499→**Enforcement**: `assert len(prompt.encode('utf-8')) <= MAX_PROMPT_BYTES` before LLM call.\n   500→\n   501→**Edge cases**:\n   502→- Single section > 60% budget: truncated to fit\n   503→- Empty sections: valid (0 bytes allocated)\n   504→- Template exceeds 5% budget: `ValueError` raised at build time\n   505→\n   506→---\n   507→\n   508→### 4.4 Deviation Registry (`deviation_registry.py`)\n   509→\n   510→**Responsibility**: FR-6, FR-10. Persistent finding store across runs.\n   511→\n   512→#### 4.4.1 Registry Schema (JSON)\n   513→\n   514→```json\n   515→{\n   516→  \"schema_version\": 1,\n   517→  \"release_id\": \"v3.0_unified-audit-gating\",\n   518→  \"spec_hash\": \"abc123...\",\n   519→  \"runs\": [\n   520→    {\n   521→      \"run_number\": 1,\n   522→      \"timestamp\": \"2026-03-19T10:00:00Z\",\n   523→      \"spec_hash\": \"abc123...\",\n   524→      \"roadmap_hash\": \"def456...\",\n   525→      \"structural_count\": 12,\n   526→      \"semantic_count\": 3,\n   527→      \"high_count\": 4,\n   528→      \"medium_count\": 8,\n   529→      \"low_count\": 3\n   530→    }\n   531→  ],\n   532→  \"findings\": {\n   533→    \"a1b2c3d4e5f67890\": {\n   534→      \"stable_id\": \"a1b2c3d4e5f67890\",\n   535→      \"dimension\": \"signatures\",\n   536→      \"rule_id\": \"phantom_id\",\n   537→      \"severity\": \"HIGH\",\n   538→      \"mismatch_type\": \"phantom_id\",\n   539→      \"spec_location\": \"FR-1.2\",\n   540→      \"description\": \"Roadmap references FR-009 which does not exist in spec\",\n   541→      \"status\": \"ACTIVE\",\n   542→      \"first_seen_run\": 1,\n   543→      \"last_seen_run\": 1,\n   544→      \"debate_verdict\": null,\n   545→      \"debate_transcript\": null\n   546→    }\n   547→  }\n   548→}\n   549→```\n   550→\n   551→#### 4.4.2 Registry API\n   552→\n   553→```python\n   554→@dataclass\n   555→class DeviationRegistry:\n   556→    \"\"\"File-backed deviation registry with stable finding IDs.\"\"\"\n   557→\n   558→    path: Path                              # JSON file path\n   559→    release_id: str\n   560→    spec_hash: str\n   561→    runs: list[dict]                        # run metadata\n   562→    findings: dict[str, dict]               # stable_id -> finding dict\n   563→\n   564→    @classmethod\n   565→    def load_or_create(cls, path: Path, release_id: str, spec_hash: str) -> DeviationRegistry:\n   566→        \"\"\"Load existing registry or create fresh one.\n   567→\n   568→        If spec_hash differs from saved → reset (new spec version, FR-6).\n   569→        \"\"\"\n   570→\n   571→    def begin_run(self, roadmap_hash: str) -> int:\n   572→        \"\"\"Start a new run. Returns run_number.\"\"\"\n   573→\n   574→    def merge_findings(\n   575→        self,\n   576→        structural: list[Finding],\n   577→        semantic: list[Finding],\n   578→        run_number: int,\n   579→    ) -> None:\n   580→        \"\"\"Merge current scan findings into registry.\n   581→\n   582→        - New findings (stable_id not in registry): append with first_seen_run\n   583→        - Known findings (stable_id exists): update last_seen_run\n   584→        - Missing findings (in registry but not in current scan): mark FIXED\n   585→        \"\"\"\n   586→\n   587→    def get_active_highs(self) -> list[dict]:\n   588→        \"\"\"Return findings with status=ACTIVE and severity=HIGH.\"\"\"\n   589→\n   590→    def get_active_high_count(self) -> int:\n   591→        \"\"\"Count of active HIGH findings (gate evaluation).\"\"\"\n   592→\n   593→    def get_prior_findings_summary(self, max_entries: int = 50) -> str:\n   594→        \"\"\"Format prior findings for semantic layer prompt (FR-10).\n   595→\n   596→        Returns formatted string: ID | severity | status | first_seen_run\n   597→        Truncates at max_entries, oldest first.\n   598→        \"\"\"\n   599→\n   600→    def update_finding_status(self, stable_id: str, status: str) -> None:\n   601→        \"\"\"Update a finding's status (FIXED, FAILED, SKIPPED).\"\"\"\n   602→\n   603→    def record_debate_verdict(\n   604→        self,\n   605→        stable_id: str,\n   606→        verdict: str,\n   607→        transcript_path: str,\n   608→    ) -> None:\n   609→        \"\"\"Record adversarial debate outcome for a finding.\"\"\"\n   610→\n   611→    def save(self) -> None:\n   612→        \"\"\"Atomic write: tmp + os.replace().\"\"\"\n   613→```\n   614→\n   615→**Key design decisions**:\n   616→- **JSON format**: Simpler than YAML for programmatic access; no PyYAML dependency for this module.\n   617→- **Spec hash reset**: When `spec_hash` changes, all findings are archived and registry starts fresh (FR-6).\n   618→- **Stable IDs**: 16-char hex hash of `(dimension, rule_id, spec_location, mismatch_type)` — collision-resistant for the expected finding cardinality (<1000).\n   619→- **Status values**: `ACTIVE`, `FIXED`, `FAILED`, `SKIPPED` — matching existing `Finding.status` but with `ACTIVE` replacing `PENDING` for registry clarity.\n   620→\n   621→> **Status compatibility note**: Both `ACTIVE` and `PENDING` are valid initial statuses in `VALID_FINDING_STATUSES`. `ACTIVE` is used by the deviation registry for findings not yet resolved; `PENDING` is the legacy pipeline default. Both represent \"not yet resolved\" and have equivalent semantics. The deviation registry uses `ACTIVE`; the existing pipeline steps 1–7 continue using `PENDING`.\n   622→\n   623→---\n   624→\n   625→### 4.5 Convergence Engine (`convergence.py`)\n   626→\n   627→**Responsibility**: FR-7, FR-8. Budget enforcement, monotonic progress (`structural_high_count` only — semantic findings do not trigger regression), regression handling.\n   628→\n   629→```python\n   630→@dataclass\n   631→class ConvergenceResult:\n   632→    \"\"\"Outcome of a convergence-controlled fidelity run.\"\"\"\n   633→    passed: bool\n   634→    run_count: int\n   635→    final_high_count: int\n   636→    progress_log: list[str]             # per-run \"{run_n_highs} → {run_n+1_highs}\"\n   637→    structural_progress_log: list[str]  # per-run \"{structural_highs_n} → {structural_highs_n+1}\"\n   638→    semantic_fluctuation_log: list[str] # per-run semantic HIGH count changes (informational)\n   639→    regression_detected: bool\n   640→    halt_reason: str | None             # None if passed\n   641→\n   642→def execute_fidelity_with_convergence(\n   643→    spec_path: Path,\n   644→    roadmap_path: Path,\n   645→    registry_path: Path,\n   646→    config: RoadmapConfig,\n   647→    max_runs: int = 3,\n   648→) -> ConvergenceResult:\n   649→    \"\"\"Run the full fidelity pipeline with convergence control.\n   650→\n   651→    Algorithm:\n   652→\n   653→    for run in 1..max_runs:\n   654→        1. Parse spec + roadmap (spec_parser)\n   655→        2. Run structural checkers (structural_checkers)\n   656→        3. Run semantic layer with structural findings as context\n   657→        4. Merge all findings into deviation registry\n   658→        5. Evaluate gate: active_high_count == 0?\n   659→           → YES: return PASS\n   660→        6. Check monotonic progress (structural findings only):\n   661→           → run_n+1.structural_high_count > run_n.structural_high_count? → REGRESSION\n   662→              (semantic fluctuations logged as warnings, never trigger regression)\n   663→              a. Spawn 3 parallel validation agents (FR-8)\n   664→              b. Merge/dedup results by stable ID\n   665→              c. Adversarial debate on each HIGH\n   666→              d. Update registry with debate verdicts\n   667→              e. Re-evaluate gate\n   668→        7. If budget remaining: run patch remediation (FR-9)\n   669→           → apply patches, re-run from step 1\n   670→\n   671→    if budget exhausted:\n   672→        return HALT with diagnostic report\n   673→    \"\"\"\n   674→```\n   675→\n   676→#### 4.5.1 Regression Detection & Parallel Validation (FR-8)\n   677→\n   678→```python\n   679→def handle_regression(\n   680→    registry: DeviationRegistry,\n   681→    spec_path: Path,\n   682→    roadmap_path: Path,\n   683→    registry_path: Path,\n   684→    config: RoadmapConfig,\n   685→) -> list[Finding]:\n   686→    \"\"\"Spawn 3 parallel validation agents in temporary directories.\n   687→\n   688→    Steps:\n   689→    1. Create 3 temporary directories with independent file copies\n   690→    2. In each temp directory, run full checker suite independently\n   691→    3. Collect all findings from all 3 agents\n   692→    4. Merge by stable_id: union of all findings\n   693→    5. Deduplicate: finding present in ≥2 agents = confirmed\n   694→    6. Write consolidated report to fidelity-regression-validation.md\n   695→    7. For each HIGH in consolidated: adversarial debate\n   696→    8. Update registry with debate verdicts\n   697→    9. Clean up temporary directories\n   698→\n   699→    Returns merged+debated findings.\n   700→    \"\"\"\n   701→```\n   702→\n   703→**Temp directory management**:\n   704→\n   705→```python\n   706→def _create_validation_dirs(\n   707→    spec_path: Path,\n   708→    roadmap_path: Path,\n   709→    registry_path: Path,\n   710→    count: int = 3,\n   711→) -> list[Path]:\n   712→    \"\"\"Create temporary directories with independent file copies.\n   713→\n   714→    Each directory gets its own copy of spec, roadmap, and registry.\n   715→    Uses tempfile.mkdtemp for OS-managed temp directory creation.\n   716→    \"\"\"\n   717→\n   718→def _cleanup_validation_dirs(dirs: list[Path]) -> None:\n   719→    \"\"\"Remove temporary validation directories.\n   720→\n   721→    Best-effort cleanup: logs warning on failure, does not raise.\n   722→    Registered as atexit fallback for crash safety.\n   723→    \"\"\"\n   724→```\n   725→\n   726→**Key design decisions**:\n   727→- **Temp directory isolation**: Each agent gets independent file copies in an OS-managed temp directory, preventing file contention (NFR-4). No git dependency required.\n   728→- **Union merge**: Any finding that appears in ANY agent's output is preserved. This is deliberately inclusive to avoid false negatives.\n   729→- **Confirmation threshold**: Findings in ≥2/3 agents are marked `confirmed=True` in the registry for auditability.\n   730→- **Counts as one run**: The entire regression flow (spawn + merge + debate) counts as a single run toward the 3-run budget.\n   731→- **Crash-safe cleanup**: `atexit.register(_cleanup_validation_dirs, dirs)` ensures temp directories are removed even on unexpected exits.\n   732→\n   733→---\n   734→\n   735→### 4.6 Patch-Based Remediation (Modified `remediate_executor.py`)\n   736→\n   737→**Responsibility**: FR-9. Replace freeform file rewrites with structured patches.\n   738→\n   739→#### 4.6.1 Patch Model\n   740→\n   741→```python\n   742→@dataclass\n   743→class RemediationPatch:\n   744→    \"\"\"MorphLLM-compatible lazy edit snippet.\"\"\"\n   745→    target_file: str\n   746→    finding_id: str\n   747→    original_code: str              # relevant section from current file\n   748→    instruction: str                # human-readable edit instruction\n   749→    update_snippet: str             # new code with // ... existing code ... markers\n   750→    rationale: str                  # why this edit is needed\n   751→\n   752→    def diff_size_ratio(self, file_content: str) -> float:\n   753→        \"\"\"Compute changed_lines / total_file_lines.\"\"\"\n   754→        total = len(file_content.splitlines())\n   755→        if total == 0:\n   756→            return 1.0\n   757→        # Count lines in update_snippet that differ from original_code\n   758→        original_lines = set(self.original_code.splitlines())\n   759→        update_lines = self.update_snippet.splitlines()\n   760→        changed = sum(1 for line in update_lines\n   761→                      if line.strip() != \"// ... existing code ...\"\n   762→                      and line not in original_lines)\n   763→        return changed / total\n   764→```\n   765→\n   766→#### 4.6.2 Patch Application Pipeline\n   767→\n   768→```python\n   769→def apply_patches(\n   770→    patches: list[RemediationPatch],\n   771→    config: PipelineConfig,\n   772→    registry: DeviationRegistry,\n   773→    diff_threshold: float = 0.30,\n   774→    allow_regeneration: bool = False,\n   775→) -> tuple[int, int]:  # (applied_count, rejected_count)\n   776→    \"\"\"Apply patches sequentially per file with diff-size guard.\n   777→\n   778→    Args:\n   779→        allow_regeneration: If True, patches exceeding diff_threshold are applied\n   780→            with a WARNING log instead of being rejected. Useful for convergence\n   781→            runs where regeneration of large sections is expected.\n   782→\n   783→    Algorithm:\n   784→    1. Group patches by target_file\n   785→    2. For each file:\n   786→       a. Create snapshot (.pre-remediate)\n   787→       b. For each patch (sequential within file):\n   788→          i.   Compute diff_size_ratio\n   789→          ii.  If ratio > threshold:\n   790→               - If allow_regeneration=True: log WARNING, proceed with application\n   791→               - If allow_regeneration=False: reject, log, mark FAILED in registry\n   792→          iii. Apply patch (MorphLLM or fallback)\n   793→          iv.  Mark FIXED in registry\n   794→       c. If any patch failed: rollback file from snapshot\n   795→    3. Return (applied, rejected) counts\n   796→    \"\"\"\n   797→\n   798→def fallback_apply(patch: RemediationPatch, file_path: Path) -> bool:\n   799→    \"\"\"Deterministic Python text replacement when MorphLLM unavailable.\n   800→\n   801→    Uses original_code as anchor:\n   802→    1. Read file content\n   803→    2. Find original_code substring (exact match)\n   804→    3. If not found: try fuzzy match (strip whitespace differences)\n   805→    4. Replace with update_snippet (stripped of // ... markers)\n   806→    5. Write back atomically\n   807→\n   808→    Returns True on success, False on anchor-not-found.\n   809→    \"\"\"\n   810→\n   811→def check_morphllm_available() -> bool:\n   812→    \"\"\"Check if MorphLLM MCP server is active at runtime.\n   813→\n   814→    Returns True if the morph-edit tool is available via MCP.\n   815→    \"\"\"\n   816→```\n   817→\n   818→**Key design decisions**:\n   819→- **Per-patch guard, not per-file**: Each individual patch is evaluated against the 30% threshold independently (resolved question #4).\n   820→- **Sequential within file**: Patches for the same file are applied one at a time to prevent ordering conflicts.\n   821→- **MorphLLM optional**: `check_morphllm_available()` probes for the MCP tool at runtime. If absent, the deterministic `fallback_apply()` is used.\n   822→- **Per-file rollback**: Existing `create_snapshots`/`restore_from_snapshots` mechanism is reused from `remediate_executor.py`.\n   823→\n   824→---\n   825→\n   826→## 5. Integration with Existing Pipeline\n   827→\n   828→### 5.1 Pipeline Step Modification\n   829→\n   830→The existing step 8 (`spec-fidelity`) becomes the entry point for the new convergence-controlled system. Steps 1–7 remain unchanged.\n   831→\n   832→**Current** (in `executor.py::_build_steps`):\n   833→```python\n   834→Step(\n   835→    id=\"spec-fidelity\",\n   836→    prompt=build_spec_fidelity_prompt(config.spec_file, merge_file),\n   837→    output_file=spec_fidelity_file,\n   838→    gate=SPEC_FIDELITY_GATE,\n   839→    ...\n   840→)\n   841→```\n   842→\n   843→**Proposed** — Step 8 construction is conditional based on convergence mode:\n   844→\n   845→```python\n   846→# In executor.py::_build_steps, step 8 construction:\n   847→if config.convergence_enabled:\n   848→    # Convergence mode: registry is authoritative (Design Principle #3)\n   849→    Step(\n   850→        id=\"spec-fidelity\",\n   851→        prompt=None,  # No LLM fidelity prompt; convergence engine handles this\n   852→        output_file=spec_fidelity_file,\n   853→        gate=None,    # No SPEC_FIDELITY_GATE; registry evaluates pass/fail\n   854→    )\n   855→else:\n   856→    # Legacy mode: SPEC_FIDELITY_GATE is authoritative\n   857→    Step(\n   858→        id=\"spec-fidelity\",\n   859→        prompt=build_spec_fidelity_prompt(config.spec_file, merge_file),\n   860→        output_file=spec_fidelity_file,\n   861→        gate=SPEC_FIDELITY_GATE,\n   862→    )\n   863→```\n   864→\n   865→**Post-step orchestration** (in `executor.py::execute_roadmap`, after steps 1-7 complete):\n   866→\n   867→```python\n   868→from .convergence import execute_fidelity_with_convergence\n   869→\n   870→result = execute_fidelity_with_convergence(\n   871→    spec_path=config.spec_file,\n   872→    roadmap_path=out / \"roadmap.md\",\n   873→    registry_path=out / \"deviation-registry.json\",\n   874→    config=config,\n   875→    max_runs=3,\n   876→)\n   877→\n   878→if not result.passed:\n   879→    # Write diagnostic report\n   880→    _write_convergence_halt_report(result, out)\n   881→    sys.exit(1)\n   882→```\n   883→\n   884→### 5.2 State Integration\n   885→\n   886→The deviation registry lives alongside `.roadmap-state.json`:\n   887→\n   888→```\n   889→output_dir/\n   890→├── .roadmap-state.json          # existing pipeline state\n   891→├── deviation-registry.json      # NEW: persistent finding registry\n   892→├── spec-fidelity.md             # existing: LLM fidelity report (now generated per-run)\n   893→├── fidelity-regression-validation.md  # NEW: regression validation report\n   894→└── roadmap.md                   # existing: merged roadmap\n   895→```\n   896→\n   897→**State file updates**: `.roadmap-state.json` gains a `fidelity_convergence` key:\n   898→\n   899→```json\n   900→{\n   901→  \"fidelity_convergence\": {\n   902→    \"status\": \"pass|fail|in_progress\",\n   903→    \"runs_completed\": 2,\n   904→    \"final_high_count\": 0,\n   905→    \"registry_path\": \"deviation-registry.json\",\n   906→    \"regression_detected\": false\n   907→  }\n   908→}\n   909→```\n   910→\n   911→### 5.3 Gate Authority Model\n   912→\n   913→The system uses **mutual exclusion** to prevent dual-authority conflicts:\n   914→\n   915→- **Convergence mode** (`convergence_enabled=True`): The `DeviationRegistry` is the sole authority for pass/fail evaluation. `SPEC_FIDELITY_GATE` is excluded from step 8. The `spec-fidelity.md` report is generated FROM registry state for human readability but is not gate-evaluated.\n   916→\n   917→- **Legacy mode** (`convergence_enabled=False`): `SPEC_FIDELITY_GATE` is the sole authority, reading `high_severity_count` from `spec-fidelity.md` frontmatter. No `DeviationRegistry` is used.\n   918→\n   919→**The two authorities never coexist in the same execution mode.** This eliminates the contradiction where the registry says PASS but the gate says FAIL (or vice versa).\n   920→\n   921→---\n   922→\n   923→## 6. Data Flow Diagram\n   924→\n   925→```\n   926→┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n   927→│                    CONVERGENCE ENGINE (max 3 runs)              │\n   928→│                                                                 │\n   929→│  ┌──────────┐   ┌──────────────────┐   ┌───────────────────┐   │\n   930→│  │ spec.md  │──→│  SPEC PARSER     │──→│ SpecData (frozen)  │   │\n   931→│  │          │   │  (spec_parser.py) │   │ RoadmapData        │   │\n   932→│  │roadmap.md│──→│                  │   │ (frozen)           │   │\n   933→│  └──────────┘   └──────────────────┘   └─────────┬─────────┘   │\n   934→│                                                   │             │\n   935→│                        ┌──────────────────────────┤             │\n   936→│                        │                          │             │\n   937→│                        ▼                          ▼             │\n   938→│  ┌─────────────────────────────┐  ┌──────────────────────────┐  │\n   939→│  │   5 STRUCTURAL CHECKERS    │  │   RESIDUAL SEMANTIC      │  │\n   940→│  │   (parallel execution)     │  │   LAYER (chunked LLM)    │  │\n   941→│  │                            │  │                          │  │\n   942→│  │   Signatures ──→ findings  │  │   Receives structural    │  │\n   943→│  │   DataModels ──→ findings  │  │   findings as context    │  │\n   944→│  │   Gates ──────→ findings   │  │   ↓                      │  │\n   945→│  │   CLI ────────→ findings   │  │   Semantic findings      │  │\n   946→│  │   NFRs ───────→ findings   │  │   ↓                      │  │\n   947→│  │                            │  │   Any HIGH?                           │   │\n   962→│  │    YES → PASS (exit convergence loop)                    │   │\n   963→│  │    NO + monotonic → REMEDIATE → next run                 │   │\n   964→│  │    NO + regression → PARALLEL VALIDATION (3 temp dirs)   │   │\n   965→│  │                      → merge → debate → update registry  │   │\n   966→│  └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   │\n   967→│                                                                 │\n   968→│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │\n   969→│  │              PATCH REMEDIATION (if needed)               │   │\n   970→│  │                                                          │   │\n   971→│  │  Active HIGHs → generate MorphLLM patches                │   │\n   972→│  │  Per-patch: diff_size_ratio ≤ 30%?                       │   │\n   973→│  │    YES → apply (MorphLLM or fallback)                    │   │\n   974→│  │    NO  → reject, mark FAILED                             │   │\n   975→│  │  Per-file rollback on failure                            │   │\n   976→│  └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   │\n   977→└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n   978→```\n   979→\n   980→---\n   981→\n   982→## 7. Error Handling & Edge Cases\n   983→\n   984→### 7.1 Parser Robustness\n   985→\n   986→| Scenario | Handling |\n   987→|----------|----------|\n   988→| Spec has no frontmatter | Return empty `SpecData.frontmatter`; checkers operate on body only |\n   989→| Malformed fenced code block | Skip block, log warning; don't crash parser |\n   990→| Requirement ID regex false positive | Checkers verify against spec-defined ID set; false positives filtered |\n   991→| Roadmap uses different heading style | Roadmap parser accepts both `## Phase` and `## N. Section` |\n   992→\n   993→### 7.2 Checker Edge Cases\n   994→\n   995→| Scenario | Handling |\n   996→|----------|----------|\n   997→| Spec has 0 function signatures | SignatureChecker returns empty findings (not an error) |\n   998→| Roadmap references IDs with different casing | Normalize to uppercase before comparison |\n   999→| File path has OS-specific separators | Normalize to forward slashes before comparison |\n  1000→\n  1001→### 7.3 Convergence Edge Cases\n  1002→\n  1003→| Scenario | Handling |\n  1004→|----------|----------|\n  1005→| Run 1 already has 0 HIGHs | PASS immediately (1-run convergence) |\n  1006→| All 3 validation agents fail | Treat as regression NOT resolved; halt with diagnostic |\n  1007→| MorphLLM patch anchor not found | Fallback apply fails → finding marked FAILED → proceeds |\n  1008→| Registry JSON corrupted | `load_or_create` catches `JSONDecodeError`, creates fresh registry |\n  1009→\n  1010→---\n  1011→\n  1012→## 8. Existing spec_parser.py\n\nPath:\n- `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/spec_parser.py`\n\nThis file is substantially implemented and aligns with Phase 1.\n\nDataclasses present:\n- `ParseWarning(category, message, location=\"\")`\n- `CodeBlock(language, content, start_line, end_line)`\n- `TableRow(cells)`\n- `MarkdownTable(heading_path, headers, rows, start_line, end_line)`\n- `FunctionSignature(name, params, return_type)`\n- `ThresholdExpression(operator, value, raw)`\n- `SpecSection(heading, heading_path, level, content, start_line, end_line)`\n- `ParseResult(frontmatter, tables, code_blocks, requirement_ids, function_signatures, literal_values, thresholds, file_paths, sections, warnings)`\n\nFunctions present:\n- `parse_frontmatter`\n- `extract_tables`\n- `_parse_table_row`\n- `extract_code_blocks`\n- `extract_requirement_ids`\n- `extract_function_signatures`\n- `extract_literal_values`\n- `extract_thresholds`\n- `extract_file_paths`\n- `extract_file_paths_from_tables`\n- `split_into_sections`\n- `parse_document`\n\nOther constants/regex:\n- `_REQUIREMENT_PATTERNS`\n- `_FUNC_SIG_RE`\n- `_LITERAL_RE`\n- `_THRESHOLD_RE`\n- `_FILE_PATH_RE`\n- `DIMENSION_SECTION_MAP`\n\nBehavior details:\n- frontmatter:\n  - tries `yaml.safe_load`\n  - falls back to line-by-line extraction with a `ParseWarning` on malformed YAML\n- tables:\n  - tracks surrounding heading path\n  - warns on missing separator row\n  - warns when row column count differs from header\n- code blocks:\n  - extracts fenced blocks with ``` or ~~~\n  - warns when language tag missing\n- requirement IDs:\n  - FR, NFR, SC, G, D families\n  - note D regex supports `D-?\\d+`, so both `D0042` and `D-0001`\n- function signatures:\n  - regex extraction from code blocks with python-ish defs\n- literal values:\n  - regex on `Literal[...]`\n- thresholds:\n  - operators `< <= > >= ==`\n  - textual forms `minimum`, `maximum`, `at least`, `at most`\n- file paths:\n  - backtick-quoted known prefixes only\n  - also scans tables for path-like cells\n- section splitting:\n  - includes frontmatter as special level 0 section\n  - includes preamble as level 0 if needed\n  - heading_path built from stack\n  - section content includes heading line itself\n\nImportant deviations from architecture-design/spec:\n- Not frozen dataclasses\n- No `SpecData` / `RoadmapData`\n- No cross-reference extraction\n- No separate `parse_spec` / `parse_roadmap`\n- `FunctionSignature.params` is a string, not structured param list\n- `SpecSection.content` includes heading line, whereas architecture doc says section body excluding heading line\n- Still, it appears intentionally scoped to Phase 1 parser foundation, not full final architecture\n\n4. code_blocks:\n        for match in _LITERAL_RE.finditer(block.content):\n            values = [v.strip().strip('\"').strip(\"'\") for v in match.group(1).split(\",\")]\n            results.append(values)\n    return results\n\n\n# ---------- Numeric Thresholds ----------\n\n_THRESHOLD_RE = re.compile(\n    r'(?:'\n    r'([<>]=?|==)\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?[%smhKMGT]*\\w*)'\n    r'|'\n    r'(minimum|maximum|at\\s+least|at\\s+most)\\s+(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?[%smhKMGT]*\\w*)'\n    r')',\n    re.IGNORECASE,\n)\n\n\ndef extract_thresholds(text: str) -> list[ThresholdExpression]:\n    \"\"\"Extract numeric threshold expressions from text.\"\"\"\n    thresholds: list[ThresholdExpression] = []\n    seen: set[str] = set()\n    for match in _THRESHOLD_RE.finditer(text):\n        raw = match.group(0).strip()\n        if raw in seen:\n            continue\n        seen.add(raw)\n        if match.group(1):\n            thresholds.append(ThresholdExpression(\n                operator=match.group(1),\n                value=match.group(2),\n                raw=raw,\n            ))\n        else:\n            thresholds.append(ThresholdExpression(\n                operator=match.group(3).lower(),\n                value=match.group(4),\n                raw=raw,\n            ))\n    return thresholds\n\n\n# ---------- File Paths ----------\n\n_FILE_PATH_RE = re.compile(\n    r'`((?:src/|tests/|docs/|scripts/|\\./)[^\\s`]+)`'\n)\n\n\ndef extract_file_paths(text: str) -> list[str]:\n    \"\"\"Extract file paths from text (backtick-quoted, starting with known prefixes).\"\"\"\n    return sorted(set(_FILE_PATH_RE.findall(text)))\n\n\ndef extract_file_paths_from_tables(tables: list[MarkdownTable]) -> list[str]:\n    \"\"\"Extract file paths from manifest tables (columns containing paths).\"\"\"\n    paths: set[str] = set()\n    path_like = re.compile(r'(?:src/|tests/|docs/|scripts/|\\./)\\S+')\n    for table in tables:\n        for row in table.rows:\n            for cell in row.cells:\n                for match in path_like.finditer(cell):\n                    # Strip backticks and trailing punctuation\n                    p = match.group(0).strip('`').rstrip('.,;:)')\n                    paths.add(p)\n    return sorted(paths)\n\n\n# ---------- Section Splitting (FR-5) ----------\n\n_HEADING_RE = re.compile(r'^(#{1,6})\\s+(.+)', re.MULTILINE)\n\n\ndef split_into_sections(text: str) -> list[SpecSection]:\n    \"\"\"Split document into sections by heading level.\n\n    Handles YAML frontmatter as level=0 section and preamble\n    (content before first heading) as level=0 section.\n    \"\"\"\n    lines = text.splitlines(keepends=True)\n    sections: list[SpecSection] = []\n    heading_stack: list[tuple[int, str]] = []\n\n    # Handle YAML frontmatter\n    fm_match = re.match(r'^---\\s*\\n(.*?\\n)---\\s*\\n', text, re.DOTALL)\n    content_start = 0\n    if fm_match:\n        fm_end = text[:fm_match.end()].count('\\n')\n        sections.append(SpecSection(\n            heading=\"frontmatter\",\n            heading_path=\"frontmatter\",\n            level=0,\n            content=fm_match.group(0),\n            start_line=1,\n            end_line=fm_end,\n        ))\n        content_start = fm_end\n\n    # Find all headings with their line positions\n    heading_positions: list[tuple[int, int, str]] = []  # (line_idx, level, title)\n    for i, line in enumerate(lines):\n        if i < content_start:\n            continue\n        m = re.match(r'^(#{1,6})\\s+(.+)', line)\n        if m:\n            heading_positions.append((i, len(m.group(1)), m.group(2).strip()))\n\n    # Handle preamble (content between frontmatter and first heading)\n    if heading_positions:\n        first_heading_line = heading_positions[0][0]\n        if first_heading_line > content_start:\n            preamble = \"\".join(lines[content_start:first_heading_line])\n            if preamble.strip():\n                sections.append(SpecSection(\n                    heading=\"preamble\",\n                    heading_path=\"preamble\",\n                    level=0,\n                    content=preamble,\n                    start_line=content_start + 1,\n                    end_line=first_heading_line,\n                ))\n    elif content_start < len(lines):\n        # No headings at all - entire content is preamble\n        preamble = \"\".join(lines[content_start:])\n        if preamble.strip():\n            sections.append(SpecSection(\n                heading=\"preamble\",\n                heading_path=\"preamble\",\n                level=0,\n                content=preamble,\n                start_line=content_start + 1,\n                end_line=len(lines),\n            ))\n\n    # Process each heading section\n    for idx, (line_idx, level, title) in enumerate(heading_positions):\n        # Update heading stack\n        heading_stack = [(l, h) for l, h in heading_stack if l < level]\n        heading_stack.append((level, title))\n        heading_path = \"/\".join(h for _, h in heading_stack)\n\n        # Determine section end\n        if idx + 1 < len(heading_positions):\n            end_idx = heading_positions[idx + 1][0]\n        else:\n            end_idx = len(lines)\n\n        content = \"\".join(lines[line_idx:end_idx])\n        sections.append(SpecSection(\n            heading=title,\n            heading_path=heading_path,\n            level=level,\n            content=content,\n            start_line=line_idx + 1,\n            end_line=end_idx,\n        ))\n\n    return sections\n\n\n# ---------- Dimension Mapping (FR-5) ----------\n\nDIMENSION_SECTION_MAP: dict[str, list[str]] = {\n    \"signatures\": [\"FR-1\", \"FR-2\", \"3. Functional Requirements\"],\n    \"data_models\": [\"4.1\", \"4.2\", \"4.3\", \"4. File Manifest\"],\n    \"gates\": [\"FR-7\", \"FR-8\", \"5.1\"],\n    \"cli\": [\"5.1\", \"CLI\", \"Commands\"],\n    \"nfrs\": [\"6.\", \"NFR\", \"Non-Functional\"],\n}\n\n\n# ---------- Full Parse ----------\n\ndef parse_document(text: str) -> ParseResult:\n    \"\"\"Parse a spec or roadmap document, extracting all structured data.\n\n    Returns a ParseResult with all extraction types populated.\n    Collects ParseWarning instances for any graceful degradation.\n    \"\"\"\n    warnings: list[ParseWarning] = []\n\n    frontmatter = parse_frontmatter(text, warnings)\n    tables = extract_tables(text, warnings)\n    code_blocks = extract_code_blocks(text, warnings)\n    requirement_ids = extract_requirement_ids(text)\n    function_signatures = extract_function_signatures(code_blocks)\n    literal_values = extract_literal_values(code_blocks)\n    thresholds = extract_thresholds(text)\n    file_paths = extract_file_paths(text)\n    file_paths_from_tables = extract_file_paths_from_tables(tables)\n    all_file_paths = sorted(set(file_paths + file_paths_from_tables))\n    sections = split_into_sections(text)\n\n    return ParseResult(\n        frontmatter=frontmatter,\n        tables=tables,\n        code_blocks=code_blocks,\n        requirement_ids=requirement_ids,\n        function_signatures=function_signatures,\n        literal_values=literal_values,\n        thresholds=thresholds,\n        file_paths=all_file_paths,\n        sections=sections,\n        warnings=warnings,\n    )\n","numLines":558,"startLine":1,"totalLines":558}}}

Convergence-specific tracking (run counting, monotonic progress)\nis handled by the convergence loop and DeviationRegistry, not by a separate\nbudget dataclass.\n\n**Preserved and coexisting**: `spec_patch.py` (the accepted-deviation workflow)\noperates in both legacy and convergence modes. In legacy mode, it patches\nspec text before fidelity comparison. In convergence mode, its `spec_hash`\ninteraction with FR-6 (registry reset on spec change) is preserved. v3.05\ndoes not modify spec_patch.py; it coexists with the new fidelity subsystem.\n\n### 1.3 v3.0 Baseline\n\nThis spec was originally drafted before v3.0 shipped. {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01PPy4rNwEC5yEHmqxM76ChP","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→---\n     2→title: \"Deterministic Spec-Fidelity Gate — Architecture Design\"\n     3→version: \"1.0.0\"\n     4→status: draft\n     5→created: 2026-03-19\n     6→source: \"/sc:design systematic deep codebase\"\n     7→parent_spec: \"deterministic-fidelity-gate-requirements.md\"\n     8→parent_feature: v3.0_unified-audit-gating\n     9→---\n    10→\n    11→# Deterministic Spec-Fidelity Gate — Architecture Design\n    12→\n    13→## 1. Design Principles\n    14→\n    15→1. **Structural-first**: ~70% of checks are deterministic Python; LLM handles only the residual semantic 30%.\n    16→2. **Immutable data flow**: Parsers produce frozen dataclasses; checkers return new `Finding` lists — no shared mutable state.\n    17→3. **Registry-centric gate**: The convergence gate reads the deviation registry, never raw scan output. `SPEC_FIDELITY_GATE` is excluded from convergence mode to prevent dual-authority conflicts (see Sec 5.3).\n    18→4. **Backward compatibility**: Pipeline steps 1–7 are untouched. The new system replaces step 8 (`spec-fidelity`) internals and adds post-step-8 orchestration.\n    19→5. **Minimal new files**: 5 new modules, 2 modified modules. No new CLI commands.\n    20→\n    21→---\n    22→\n    23→## 2. Module Map\n    24→\n    25→### 2.1 New Modules\n    26→\n    27→| Module | Location | Responsibility | FR |\n    28→|--------|----------|----------------|----|\n    29→| `spec_parser.py` | `cli/roadmap/spec_parser.py` | Parse spec + roadmap into structured `SpecData` / `RoadmapData` | FR-2 |\n    30→| `structural_checkers.py` | `cli/roadmap/structural_checkers.py` | 5 checker callables + registry + severity rule tables | FR-1, FR-3 |\n    31→| `semantic_layer.py` | `cli/roadmap/semantic_layer.py` | Chunked LLM residual pass + adversarial debate hook | FR-4, FR-5 |\n    32→| `deviation_registry.py` | `cli/roadmap/deviation_registry.py` | File-backed JSON registry with stable IDs, run metadata | FR-6, FR-10 |\n    33→| `convergence.py` | `cli/roadmap/convergence.py` | 3-run budget, monotonic progress (structural_high_count only), regression detection | FR-7, FR-8 |\n    34→\n    35→### 2.2 Modified Modules\n    36→\n    37→| Module | Change | FR |\n    38→|--------|--------|----|\n    39→| `executor.py` | Replace `spec-fidelity` step construction; add convergence loop after step 8 | FR-7 |\n    40→| `remediate_executor.py` | Add MorphLLM patch format + diff-size guard + fallback applicator | FR-9 |\n    41→\n    42→### 2.3 Unchanged Modules\n    43→\n    44→Steps 1–7 (`prompts.py` build_extract/generate/diff/debate/score/merge/test_strategy), `gates.py` (existing gate definitions), `fidelity.py` (Severity enum + FidelityDeviation — retained, extended), `spec_patch.py` (accepted deviation workflow), `models.py` (Finding dataclass — extended, not replaced).\n    45→\n    46→---\n    47→\n    48→## 3. Data Model\n    49→\n    50→### 3.1 Spec Parser Output (`spec_parser.py`)\n    51→\n    52→```python\n    53→from __future__ import annotations\n    54→from dataclasses import dataclass, field\n    55→from typing import Literal\n    56→\n    57→@dataclass(frozen=True)\n    58→class FunctionSignature:\n    59→    \"\"\"Extracted Python function signature from fenced code block.\"\"\"\n    60→    name: str\n    61→    params: list[str]           # parameter names (no types)\n    62→    return_type: str | None     # return annotation string or None\n    63→    source_section: str         # heading path where found, e.g. \"3.1/FR-1\"\n    64→\n    65→@dataclass(frozen=True)\n    66→class RequirementID:\n    67→    \"\"\"A requirement identifier extracted from spec text.\"\"\"\n    68→    id: str                     # e.g. \"FR-1.2\", \"NFR-3\", \"SC-1\", \"G-2\", \"D5\"\n    69→    family: str                 # e.g. \"FR\", \"NFR\", \"SC\", \"G\", \"D\"\n    70→    source_section: str\n    71→\n    72→@dataclass(frozen=True)\n    73→class FileManifestEntry:\n    74→    \"\"\"A file path from a spec manifest table (Sec 4.1, 4.2, 4.3).\"\"\"\n    75→    path: str                   # e.g. \"src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/spec_parser.py\"\n    76→    description: str\n    77→    source_section: str\n    78→\n    79→@dataclass(frozen=True)\n    80→class ThresholdExpression:\n    81→    \"\"\"A numeric threshold from spec text, e.g. '< 5s', '>= 90%'.\"\"\"\n    82→    raw: str                    # original text\n    83→    operator: str               # '<', '<=', '>', '>=', '=='\n    84→    value: float\n    85→    unit: str                   # 's', '%', 'KB', '' etc.\n    86→    source_section: str\n    87→\n    88→@dataclass(frozen=True)\n    89→class EnumLiteral:\n    90→    \"\"\"A Literal[...] enum value extracted from a fenced code block.\"\"\"\n    91→    type_name: str              # e.g. \"enforcement_tier\"\n    92→    values: tuple[str, ...]     # e.g. (\"STRICT\", \"STANDARD\", \"LIGHT\", \"EXEMPT\")\n    93→    source_section: str\n    94→\n    95→@dataclass(frozen=True)\n    96→class CrossReference:\n    97→    \"\"\"A cross-section reference extracted from spec text.\"\"\"\n    98→    from_section: str           # section containing the reference\n    99→    to_section: str             # section being referenced\n   100→    context: str                # surrounding text snippet\n   101→\n   102→@dataclass(frozen=True)\n   103→class SpecSection:\n   104→    \"\"\"A parsed top-level section of the spec.\"\"\"\n   105→    heading: str                # e.g. \"3. Functional Requirements\"\n   106→    heading_path: str           # e.g. \"3\"\n   107→    level: int                  # heading level (2 = ##)\n   108→    content: str                # raw markdown content\n   109→    byte_size: int              # len(content.encode('utf-8'))\n   110→\n   111→@dataclass(frozen=True)\n   112→class SpecData:\n   113→    \"\"\"Complete structured extraction from a spec document.\"\"\"\n   114→    frontmatter: dict[str, str]\n   115→    sections: tuple[SpecSection, ...]\n   116→    signatures: tuple[FunctionSignature, ...]\n   117→    requirement_ids: tuple[RequirementID, ...]\n   118→    file_manifest: tuple[FileManifestEntry, ...]\n   119→    thresholds: tuple[ThresholdExpression, ...]\n   120→    enum_literals: tuple[EnumLiteral, ...]\n   121→    cross_references: tuple[CrossReference, ...]\n   122→\n   123→    # Derived lookup indexes (computed in __post_init__ of mutable builder)\n   124→    section_by_heading: dict[str, SpecSection] = field(default_factory=dict)\n   125→    ids_by_family: dict[str, frozenset[str]] = field(default_factory=dict)\n   126→\n   127→@dataclass(frozen=True)\n   128→class RoadmapData:\n   129→    \"\"\"Structured extraction from a roadmap document.\"\"\"\n   130→    frontmatter: dict[str, str]\n   131→    sections: tuple[SpecSection, ...]      # reuse SpecSection for heading+content\n   132→    referenced_ids: frozenset[str]         # all FR-*, NFR-*, etc. found in text\n   133→    file_paths: frozenset[str]             # all file paths found in tasks\n   134→    function_names: frozenset[str]         # Design Principles\n\n1. **Structural-first**: ~70% of checks are deterministic Python; LLM handles only the residual semantic 30%.\n2. **Immutable data flow**: Parsers produce frozen dataclasses; checkers return new `Finding` lists — no shared mutable state.\n3. **Registry-centric gate**: The convergence gate reads the deviation registry, never raw scan output. `SPEC_FIDELITY_GATE` is excluded from convergence mode to prevent dual-authority conflicts (see Sec 5.3).\n4. **Backward compatibility**: Pipeline steps 1–7 are untouched. The new system replaces step 8 (`spec-fidelity`) internals and adds post-step-8 orchestration.\n5. **Minimal new files**: 5 new modules, 2 modified modules. No new CLI commands.\n\n---\n\n## 2. Module Map\n\n### 2.1 New Modules\n\n| Module | Location | Responsibility | FR |\n|--------|----------|----------------|----|\n| `spec_parser.py` | `cli/roadmap/spec_parser.py` | Parse spec + roadmap into structured `SpecData` / `RoadmapData` | FR-2 |\n| `structural_checkers.py` | `cli/roadmap/structural_checkers.py` | 5 checker callables + registry + severity rule tables | FR-1, FR-3 |\n| `semantic_layer.py` | `cli/roadmap/semantic_layer.py` | Chunked LLM residual pass + adversarial debate hook | FR-4, FR-5 |\n| `deviation_registry.py` | `cli/roadmap/deviation_registry.py` | File-backed JSON registry with stable IDs, run metadata | FR-6, FR-10 |\n| `convergence.py` | `cli/roadmap/convergence.py` | 3-run budget, monotonic progress (structural_high_count only), regression detection | FR-7, FR-8 |\n\n### 2.2 Modified Modules\n\n| Module | Change | FR |\n|--------|--------|----|\n| `executor.py` | Replace `spec-fidelity` step construction; add convergence loop after step 8 | FR-7 |\n| `remediate_executor.py` | Add MorphLLM patch format + diff-size guard + fallback applicator | FR-9 |\n\n### 2.3 Unchanged Modules\n\nSteps 1–7 (`prompts.py` build_extract/generate/diff/debate/score/merge/test_strategy), `gates.py` (existing gate definitions), `fidelity.py` (Severity enum + FidelityDeviation — retained, extended), `spec_patch.py` (accepted deviation workflow), `models.py` (Finding dataclass — extended, not replaced).\n\n---\n\n## 3. Data Model\n\n### 3.1 Spec Parser Output (`spec_parser.py`)\n\n```python\nfrom __future__ import annotations\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass, field\nfrom typing import Literal\n\n@dataclass(frozen=True)\nclass FunctionSignature:\n    \"\"\"Extracted Python function signature from fenced code block.\"\"\"\n    name: str\n    params: list[str]           # parameter names (no types)\n    return_type: str | None     # return annotation string or None\n    source_section: str         # heading path where found, e.g. \"3.1/FR-1\"\n\n@dataclass(frozen=True)\nclass RequirementID:\n    \"\"\"A requirement identifier extracted from spec text.\"\"\"\n    id: str                     # e.g. \"FR-1.2\", \"NFR-3\", \"SC-1\", \"G-2\", \"D5\"\n    family: str                 # e.g. \"FR\", \"NFR\", \"SC\", \"G\", \"D\"\n    source_section: str\n\n@dataclass(frozen=True)\nclass FileManifestEntry:\n    \"\"\"A file path from a spec manifest table (Sec 4.1, 4.2, 4.3).\"\"\"\n    path: str                   # e.g. \"src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/spec_parser.py\"\n    description: str\n    source_section: str\n\n@dataclass(frozen=True)\nclass ThresholdExpression:\n    \"\"\"A numeric threshold from spec text, e.g. '< 5s', '>= 90%'.\"\"\"\n    raw: str                    # original text\n    operator: str               # '<', '<=', '>', '>=', '=='\n    value: float\n    unit: str                   # 's', '%', 'KB', '' etc.\n    source_section: str\n\n@dataclass(frozen=True)\nclass EnumLiteral:\n    \"\"\"A Literal[...] enum value extracted from a fenced code block.\"\"\"\n    type_name: str              # e.g. \"enforcement_tier\"\n    values: tuple[str, ...]     # e.g. (\"STRICT\", \"STANDARD\", \"LIGHT\", \"EXEMPT\")\n    source_section: str\n\n@dataclass(frozen=True)\nclass CrossReference:\n    \"\"\"A cross-section reference extracted from spec text.\"\"\"\n    from_section: str           # section containing the reference\n    to_section: str             # section being referenced\n    context: str                # surrounding text snippet\n\n@dataclass(frozen=True)\nclass SpecSection:\n    \"\"\"A parsed top-level section of the spec.\"\"\"\n    heading: str                # e.g. \"3. Functional Requirements\"\n    heading_path: str           # e.g. \"3\"\n    level: int                  # heading level (2 = ##)\n    content: str                # raw markdown content\n    byte_size: int              # len(content.encode('utf-8'))\n\n@dataclass(frozen=True)\nclass SpecData:\n    \"\"\"Complete structured extraction from a spec document.\"\"\"\n    frontmatter: dict[str, str]\n    sections: tuple[SpecSection, ...]\n    signatures: tuple[FunctionSignature, ...]\n    requirement_ids: tuple[RequirementID, ...]\n    file_manifest: tuple[FileManifestEntry, ...]\n    thresholds: tuple[ThresholdExpression, ...]\n    enum_literals: tuple[EnumLiteral, ...]\n    cross_references: tuple[CrossReference, ...]\n\n    # Derived lookup indexes (computed in __post_init__ of mutable builder)\n    section_by_heading: dict[str, SpecSection] = field(default_factory=dict)\n    ids_by_family: dict[str, frozenset[str]] = field(default_factory=dict)\n\n@dataclass(frozen=True)\nclass RoadmapData:\n    \"\"\"Structured extraction from a roadmap document.\"\"\"\n    frontmatter: dict[str, str]\n    sections: tuple[SpecSection, ...]      # reuse SpecSection for heading+content\n    referenced_ids: frozenset[str]         # all FR-*, NFR-*, etc. found in text\n    file_paths: frozenset[str]             # all file paths found in tasks\n    function_names: frozenset[str]         # function/method names in task descriptions\n    field_references: frozenset[str]       # dataclass field names referenced\n    gate_params: frozenset[str]            # Step(...) parameter names referenced\n```\n\n**Parser functions** (all pure, no I/O beyond reading the two input files):\n\n```python\ndef parse_spec(spec_path: Path) -> SpecData: ...\ndef parse_roadmap(roadmap_path: Path) -> RoadmapData: ...\n```\n\n**Implementation notes**:\n- YAML frontmatter: `yaml.safe_load` on `---` delimited block (reuse `_extract_frontmatter` pattern from `spec_patch.py`)\n- Markdown tables: regex split on `|` with header row detection\n- Fenced code blocks: `^```python` … `^```\\n` regex, then `ast.parse` for signatures\n- Requirement IDs: `re.findall(r'(?:FR|NFR|SC|G|D)-?\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)*', text)`\n- `Literal[...]`: regex on `Literal\\[([^\\]]+)\\]` within fenced blocks\n- Thresholds: regex `(<=?|>=?|==)\\s*([\\d.]+)\\s*(%|s|ms|KB|MB|)?`\n- Cross-references: regex for `See (?:section |§)(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)*)` and `FR-\\d+` in non-home sections\n- Section splitting: `^## \\d+\\.` regex on spec; `^## ` on roadmap\n\n---\n\n### 3.2 Structural Finding Model\n\nExtends the existing `Finding` dataclass in `models.py`:\n\n```python\n# Addition to models.py (or new field in Finding)\n# No new class needed — Finding already has all required fields.\n# New fields added:\n\n@dataclass\nclass Finding:\n    # ... existing fields ...\n    rule_id: str = \"\"           # e.g. \"SIG-MISSING-FUNC\", \"DM-PATH-PREFIX\"\n    spec_quote: str = \"\"        # verbatim spec text\n    roadmap_quote: str = \"\"     # Missing function check\n   309→        # 3. Parameter arity check\n   310→        return findings\n   311→```\n   312→\n   313→**2. Thread pool avoids serialization overhead.\n   393→- **No shared mutable state**: Each checker receives the same frozen `SpecData`/`RoadmapData` and returns its own list (NFR-4).\n   394→- **Rule tables in code**: `SeverityRuleTable` dicts are module-level constants, not prompt text (FR-3).\n   395→\n   396→---\n   397→\n   398→### 4.3 Residual Semantic Layer (`semantic_layer.py`)\n   399→"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"1241db92-4182-4bac-88d0-fdc66073fffe","uuid":"cecf40b4-b4ca-4358-9be4-88d3cbbdd301","timestamp":"2026-03-20T20:23:57.699Z","tool_use_result":{"type":"text","file":{"filePath":"/config/workspace/IronClaude/.dev/releases/current/v3.05_DeterministicFidelityGates/architecture-design.md","content":"SeverityLevel = Lit[\"HIGH\", \"MEDIUM\", \"LOW\"]\n\n@dataclass(frozen=True)\nclass SeverityRule:\n    \"\"\"One row in a checker's severity rule table.\"\"\"\n    dimension: str          # e.g. \"signatures\"\n    mismatch_type: str      # e.g. \"function_missing\"\n    severity: SeverityLevel\n    description: str        # human-readable rule description\n\n# Type alias for the rule table\nSeverityRuleTable = dict[str, SeverityLevel]  # key: mismatch_type -> severity\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Component Architecture\n\n### 4.1 Spec Parser (`spec_parser.py`)\n\n**Responsibility**: FR-2. Read spec and roadmap files, return `SpecData` and `RoadmapData`.\n\n```\nInput:  spec_path: Path, roadmap_path: Path\nOutput: SpecData, RoadmapData\nI/O:    Reads 2 files (the only I/O in the entire checker pipeline)\n```\n\n**Key design decisions**:\n- **Single point of file I/O**: All downstream components receive parsed data, never file paths.\n- **Frozen dataclasses**: Parser output is immutable — checkers cannot accidentally mutate shared state (NFR-4).\n- **Section-level chunking**: Each `SpecSection` tracks its byte size for prompt budgeting (NFR-3).\n- **Reference graph**: `cross_references` enables supplementary section injection per checker.\n\n**Section→Dimension mapping** (FR-5):\n\n```python\n# Static mapping: which spec sections feed which checker dimension\nDIMENSION_SECTIONS: dict[str, list[str]] = {\n    \"signatures\":  [\"3\"],           # Sec 3: Functional Requirements\n    \"data_models\": [\"4.1\", \"4.2\", \"4.3\"],  # Sec 4: File manifests\n    \"gates\":       [\"3\", \"4\"],      # FR + data model gates\n    \"cli\":         [\"5.1\"],         # Sec 5: CLI options\n    \"nfrs\":        [\"6\"],           # Sec 6: Non-functional requirements\n}\n\ndef get_sections_for_dimension(\n    dimension: str,\n    spec: SpecData,\n) -> list[SpecSection]:\n    \"\"\"Return primary + supplementary sections for a checker dimension.\n\n    Primary sections come from DIMENSION_SECTIONS.\n    Supplementary sections come from cross_references that link\n    from primary sections to other sections.\n    \"\"\"\n```\n\n---\n\n### 4.2 Structural Checkers (`structural_checkers.py`)\n\n**Responsibility**: FR-1, FR-3. Five independent checker callables, each producing `list[Finding]`.\n\n#### 4.2.1 Checker Protocol\n\n```python\nfrom typing import Protocol\n\nclass StructuralChecker(Protocol):\n    \"\"\"Protocol for all structural checkers.\"\"\"\n\n    dimension: str\n    rules: SeverityRuleTable\n\n    def check(self, spec: SpecData, roadmap: RoadmapData) -> list[Finding]:\n        \"\"\"Run deterministic checks, return findings with rule-based severity.\"\"\"\n        ...\n```\n\n#### 4.2.2 Five Checker Implementations\n\n**1. SignatureChecker** (dimension: `\"signatures\"`, ~80% structural)\n\n```python\nclass SignatureChecker:\n    dimension = \"signatures\"\n    rules: SeverityRuleTable = {\n        \"phantom_id\":        \"HIGH\",    # Roadmap references ID not in spec\n        \"function_missing\":  \"HIGH\",    # Spec function absent from roadmap\n        \"param_arity\":       \"MEDIUM\",  # Parameter count mismatch\n        \"id_missing\":        \"MEDIUM\",  # Spec ID not referenced in roadmap\n    }\n\n    def check(self, spec: SpecData, roadmap: RoadmapData) -> list[Finding]:\n        findings = []\n        # 1. Phantom ID check: roadmap IDs ⊄ spec IDs\n        spec_ids = set()\n        for req in spec.requirement_ids:\n            spec_ids.add(req.id)\n        phantom = roadmap.referenced_ids - spec_ids\n        for pid in sorted(phantom):\n            findings.append(Finding(\n                dimension=self.dimension,\n                rule_id=\"phantom_id\",\n                severity=\"HIGH\",\n                ...\n            ))\n        # 2. Missing function check\n        # 3. Parameter arity check\n        return findings\n```\n\n**2. DataModelChecker** (dimension: `\"data_models\"`, ~85% structural)\n\n```python\nrules = {\n    \"file_missing\":      \"HIGH\",    # Required spec file missing from roadmap\n    \"path_prefix\":       \"HIGH\",    # File path prefix mismatch\n    \"enum_uncovered\":    \"MEDIUM\",  # Enum literal not covered\n    \"field_missing\":     \"MEDIUM\",  # Dataclass field not referenced\n}\n```\n\n**3. GateChecker** (dimension: `\"gates\"`, ~65% structural)\n\n```python\nrules = {\n    \"frontmatter_field\": \"HIGH\",    # Required frontmatter field not covered\n    \"step_param\":        \"MEDIUM\",  # Step parameter missing\n    \"ordering\":          \"MEDIUM\",  # Ordering constraint violated\n}\n```\n\n**4. CLIChecker** (dimension: `\"cli\"`, ~75% structural)\n\n```python\nrules = {\n    \"mode_uncovered\":    \"MEDIUM\",  # Config mode not covered\n    \"default_mismatch\":  \"MEDIUM\",  # Default value mismatch\n}\n```\n\n**5. NFRChecker** (dimension: `\"nfrs\"`, ~55% structural)\n\n```python\nrules = {\n    \"threshold_contradicted\": \"HIGH\",    # Numeric threshold contradicted\n    \"security_missing\":       \"HIGH\",    # Security primitive missing\n    \"dependency_violated\":    \"HIGH\",    # Dependency direction violated\n    \"coverage_mismatch\":      \"MEDIUM\",  # Coverage threshold mismatch\n}\n```\n\n#### 4.2.3 Checker Registry\n\n```python\n# Module-level registry\nCHECKER_REGISTRY: dict[str, StructuralChecker] = {\n    \"signatures\":  SignatureChecker(),\n    \"data_models\": DataModelChecker(),\n    \"gates\":       GateChecker(),\n    \"cli\":         CLIChecker(),\n    \"nfrs\":        NFRChecker(),\n}\n\ndef run_all_checkers(\n    spec: SpecData,\n    roadmap: RoadmapData,\n) -> list[Finding]:\n    \"\"\"Execute all checkers in parallel, merge findings.\"\"\"\n    from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed\n\n    all_findings: list[Finding] = []\n    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as pool:\n        futures = {\n            pool.submit(checker.check, spec, roadmap): dim\n            for dim, checker in CHECKER_REGISTRY.items()\n        }\n        for future in as_completed(futures):\n            all_findings.extend(future.result())\n\n    # Assign stable IDs\n    for f in all_findings:\n        f.stable_id = compute_stable_id(\n            f.dimension, f.rule_id, f.location, f.rule_id\n        )\n\n    return all_findings\n```\n\n**Key design decisions**:\n- **ThreadPoolExecutor** not ProcessPoolExecutor: checkers are CPU-light (string matching), not CPU-bound. Thread pool avoids serialization overhead.\n- **No shared mutable state**: Each checker receives the same frozen `SpecData`/`RoadmapData` and returns its own list (NFR-4).\n- **Rule tables in code**: `SeverityRuleTable` dicts are module-level constants, not prompt text (FR-3).\n\n---\n\n### 4.3 Residual Semantic Layer (`semantic_layer.py`)\n","numLines":200,"startLine":200,"totalLines":1106}}}

check_nfrs(spec_path: str, roadmap_path: str) -> list[Finding]:\n    \"\"\"NFRs checker: verifies numeric thresholds, security primitives, dependency rules.\n\n    Machine keys:
